For anyone who is curious about the "workplace drama" here is the translation:  First Interaction  Man :  Arya (or Anya sorry couldn't make out, girl's name) are you mad? you... Girl : Its because of the tax it's going so high.. Man : Yes  After that as Ryan leaves,   Man : Why do you always charge wrong? (Something like that couldn't hear it properly)   Girl : (Flustered) It's because....(some excuses about how she doesn't know the machine operates that well)   Second Interaction  When the girl tells Ryan to go to that aisle, the man, presumably her father from what i could tell from their interactions, comes in to say:  Man : The tape was right here somewhere......(when he finds it) What is this? (directed towards his daughter(?) not Ryan) Girl : (in a cliche sullen and quite voice) Don't know...  To anyone curios the language spoken was Hindi, one of the major languages of the Indian subcontinent. It was a normal, albeit a bit rude as the man appeared to be annoyed with the girl, interaction between a father and his daughter.
